Used for truncation decisions during follower recovery.\\n- **`storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/LeaderEpochCheckpointFile.java`**: Handles reading/writing the leader epoch checkpoint file on disk (format: version + list of epoch/offset pairs).\\n- **`storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/EpochEntry.java`**: Data class representing a (epoch, startOffset) entry in the epoch cache.\\n\\n## LogStartOffset Tracking\\n- **`storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogStartOffsetIncrementReason.java`**: Enum for the reason a log start offset is incremented (leader offset incremented, segment deletion, etc.).\\n- **`storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/UnifiedLog.java`**: Contains `maybeIncrementLogStartOffset` and `maybeIncrementLocalLogStartOffset` which update the log start offset and checkpoint it. The `AlterPartitionListener` trait is also defined here with `markIsrExpand()` and `markIsrShrink()` callbacks.\\n- **`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaManager.scala`**: Schedules periodic `maybeShrinkIsr()` calls on all online partitions. Responsible for sending AlterPartition requests to the controller when ISR changes are requested by a partition leader.\\n- **`core/src/main/java/kafka/server/TierStateMachine.java`**: State machine for tiered storage that interacts with leader epoch checkpoints during log segment tiering.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":13121,"cache_read_input_tokens":40571,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":13121,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":8,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"906965d5-d184-4147-bc55-7551946a4436","uuid":"b350cb9a-35f4-456f-bcb0-ea1d1dd4f6c8"}
